# Comments for Question 2, LLM=GLM-4.5

== Grader: Claude 3.7 Sonnet ==
  * grade_story_1.txt (grade=5.8)
    The plot has a clear arc—from finding coordinates to discovering the library to unraveling knots representing fears—but relies too heavily on convenient symbolism. The connection between garage sales and pyramid discovery feels underdeveloped and implausible. While the metaphorical knots provide structure, the resolution comes too easily for a character supposedly plagued by lifelong phobias, undermining the stakes and tension.

  * grade_story_0.txt (grade=7.1)
    The plot has a clear arc with logical cause-effect relationships. The spy's mission to unite humans and monsters through forgotten promises drives the narrative purposefully. The stained glass lamp effectively serves as both tool and symbol. However, the resolution feels rushed and too convenient—the monster's immediate positive response undermines potential tension, and the transition from conflict to resolution lacks the necessary complexity for a truly satisfying payoff.

  * grade_story_10.txt (grade=5.8)
    The plot connects the beginning (isolated duelist) to the end (man at peace) with reasonable coherence, but relies too heavily on telling rather than showing the transformation. The elasticizing action serves more as a metaphorical device than a plot driver. While the chest's revelation provides a turning point, the resolution feels too neat and simplistic for such profound emotional work, lacking the necessary complexity or resistance to make the arc believable.

  * grade_story_100.txt (grade=4.8)
    The plot structure suffers from vagueness about what the "cosmic deception" actually is, making the stakes unclear. While following moon paths drives movement, the resolution feels rushed and too convenient—simply holding up glowing pennies immediately solves the central conflict. The cause-effect relationship between the pennies' resonance and the shattering of illusion lacks sufficient setup. The story attempts an arc but the resolution feels unearned given the minimal obstacles encountered.
